---

### Phase Details (v58.0)

#### Phase 363: PREP — Scope Freeze, Inventory & Run Scaffold

**Goal**: The audit subject is frozen and the run is set up so phases 364-369 can execute hands-off and resumably with zero re-attestation drift: `FROZEN_SHA` is pinned, the context-pack is rebuilt + every `file:line` re-attested against it, the complete source-of-truth inventory for all four web sections is enumerated, the cohesive static-site shell exists under `audit/site/`, and the autonomous + budget-paced + checkpoint/resume run contract is locked.
**Requirements**: PREP-01, PREP-02, PREP-03, OPS-01, OPS-02
**Success criteria**:

1. `FROZEN_SHA` pinned to the v57 contract-frozen HEAD; `audit-v52/` `scope.txt`/`targets.md`/`hot-surfaces.md` rebuilt with `AfKing.sol`→`GameAfkingModule.sol` + `DegenerusGameBingoModule.sol` reconciled and 0 stale `file:line` refs.
2. The four enumerations (player-facing functions · RNG-interacting variables · ETH inflow/pool/outflow sites · `advanceGame` stages) exist as explicit lists, with any coverage gap logged (no silent truncation).
3. `audit/site/` opens from a local file with a working shared nav/tabs shell + a searchable-table component, no build step / framework / CDN.
4. The resumable run contract is written down: the harness config (`concurrency: 1`, small batches), the per-phase checkpoint/persist + commit convention, and the ~45%-weekly / 24h / no-5h-cap pacing rule.

#### Phase 364: RNGSAFE — Player-Function RNG-Safety Page + Sanity/Comment Check

**Goal**: A reader can see every player-facing function, understand what it does, and read a cited reason WHY it cannot influence any RNG-dependent variable between request and resolution — and every behavior↔name/comment mismatch (a real-bug class, e.g. a BURNIE-burning buy that queues zero tickets) is surfaced as a finding.
**Requirements**: RNGSAFE-01, RNGSAFE-02, RNGSAFE-03
**Success criteria**:

1. Every player-facing function from the 363 enumeration has a row (contract · signature · what-it-does · gating); 0 unlisted, deliberate exclusions noted.
2. Each row carries an RNG-safety verdict + cited reasoning; any function able to touch a participating slot in the freeze window is escalated to a finding.
3. The sanity/comment check is applied to every row; each behavior↔comment mismatch is recorded as a severity-classified finding with a fix sketch.
4. The RNG-Safety section renders in the site as a searchable/filterable table.

#### Phase 365: RNGVAR — RNG-Variable Freeze Invariant Table

**Goal**: A reader can see every variable that feeds RNG and a cited proof of why it cannot be modified between RNG request and resolution.
**Requirements**: RNGVAR-01, RNGVAR-02, RNGVAR-03
**Success criteria**:

1. Every RNG-participating variable is enumerated with its location + the RNG outputs it feeds.
2. Each variable's writer set is enumerated and each writer shown lock-gated or window-unreachable, cited to `file:line`; any window-mutating writer escalated to a finding.
3. The RNG-Variable Freeze table renders in the site (variable → outputs → writers → freeze-gate), searchable.

#### Phase 366: ETHFLOW — ETH Flow Chart

**Goal**: A reader can follow every ETH wei from where it enters, through the pools, to where it leaves — and the conservation/solvency invariant is visible at each hop.
**Requirements**: ETHFLOW-01, ETHFLOW-02, ETHFLOW-03
**Success criteria**:

1. Every ETH inflow is traced to its destination pool/ledger with an entry `file:line`.
2. Pool cycling + every outflow is traced with the conservation/solvency invariant noted per hop; any leak/mismatch escalated to a finding.
3. A readable ETH-flow diagram (sources/pools/sinks + labeled edges) renders in the site, each edge backed by a `file:line`.

#### Phase 367: GASCEIL — advanceGame Gas-Ceiling Table

**Goal**: A reader can see the theoretical worst-case gas of each `advanceGame` stage and whether it stays under the 16.7M per-tx cap.
**Requirements**: GASCEIL-01, GASCEIL-02, GASCEIL-03
**Success criteria**:

1. `advanceGame` is decomposed into ordered stages, each with its bounding loop + iteration cap.
2. Worst-case max gas per stage is derived (marginal × ceiling) with explicit bounding assumptions (worst-case branch, not typical seed).
3. The gas-ceiling table renders with a per-stage verdict vs the 16,777,216 cap; any stage that could approach/exceed it is escalated to a finding.

#### Phase 368: FORENSIC — BURNIE Ticket-Mint Regression Forensic (side track)

**Goal**: The "BURNIE burned but no tickets queued" regression is root-caused to a commit and explained, with a regression-test recommendation so it can't recur silently.
**Requirements**: FORENSIC-01, FORENSIC-02
**Success criteria**:

1. The introducing commit SHA + era/refactor is identified via git history.
2. A short root-cause note explains why no test caught it + recommends the specific regression test (post-buy ticket-queue-growth assertion on the coin path).

#### Phase 369: TERMINAL — External Corroboration + Site Assembly + FINDINGS-v58.0 + Closure

**Goal**: The artifacts are corroborated by a targeted external second opinion, assembled into one cohesive shippable site, and every finding is consolidated into `audit/FINDINGS-v58.0.md`; the milestone closes with a signal.
**Requirements**: XMODEL-01, SITE-01, AUDIT-01
**Success criteria**:

1. ~5 area prompts × 2 models run (after a council PONG smoke-test); each external claim adjudicated by Claude and folded into the artifacts/FINDINGS.
2. The four sections assemble into ONE cohesive navigable site under `audit/site/` (shared nav, dark aesthetic, searchable tables, embedded ETH-flow diagram, opens with no server/build).

## Phase Details (v57.0)

### Phase 358: SPEC — Design-Lock + Freeze/Solvency Re-Attestation + Call-Graph Attestation

**Goal**: The v57.0 open design decisions are settled in writing so the IMPL phase authors a fully reconciled diff with zero "by construction" assumptions, and the load-bearing freeze-safety + byte-preservation are designed BEFORE any code: the WWXRP per-bracket rationing key + operator-recipient policy (WWXRP-02 design half), the terminal-decimator design decisions (TDEC-02 SPEC half: effective-streak source, the bucket-improvement/promotion rule + keep-vs-re-derive-`subBucket`, the `uint88` overflow policy, double-count-vs-burn-time-`multBps`, shields consume-vs-read) + the freeze-safety re-proof under the bucket-promotion allowance (TDEC-03 SPEC half), and the UDVT width/byte-preservation discipline (the per-site cast/keep/widen decision matrix) are LOCKED; the BURNIE coin-buy ticket-queue Critical fix is design-locked (BURNIE-03 — the `_purchaseCoinFor` queue-on-return algorithm + the MINT_BURNIE burn-rebate mechanic [full-cost gate, deferred net burn] + the BATCH-01 reconciliation + the freeze/solvency framing); the RNG-freeze-intact + SOLVENCY-01-byte-untouched properties are re-attested on paper; and every cited `file:line` is grep-verified against the v56.0 HEAD `1e7a646d` — paper-only, zero `contracts/*.sol`.
**Type**: SPEC
**Depends on**: Nothing (first v57.0 phase; consumes the v56.0 closure HEAD `1e7a646d` as the frozen audit baseline, plus the design-lock inputs `.planning/PLAN-WWXRP-JACKPOT-WHALEPASS.md` + `.planning/PLAN-TERMINAL-DECIMATOR-STREAK-BOOST.md` + the `type-day-udvt-post-v56-seed` + `handlepurchase-burnie-flip-batching-post-v56-seed` memories; the BURNIE fix was found+verified mid-358 against `1e7a646d`)
**Requirements**: WWXRP-02, TDEC-02, TDEC-03, BURNIE-03, SALVAGE-02, CANCEL-02
**Success Criteria** (what must be TRUE):

  1. The WWXRP whale-halfpass design is locked (WWXRP-02 design half) — the per-10-level-bracket rationing key is settled (`level/10`, a per-bracket award flag, NOT a global 0→5 lifetime cap), the operator-placed-bet recipient policy is decided (pass to `player` = bet owner vs operator) and whether one player may win multiple brackets across the game is settled (default allow — naturally rationed), the new `wwxrpJackpotWhalePass*` per-bracket storage shape is fixed, and the freeze-safe/cheap properties (writes only an RNG-insensitive counter gated by the already-committed `s==9`, reuses `claimWhalePass`, short-circuits on non-jackpot spins) are re-attested on paper — recorded for the IMPL (WWXRP-01 is owned at IMPL; its design is fixed here).
  2. The terminal-decimator design decisions are locked (TDEC-02 SPEC half) — the effective-streak source is `getPlayerQuestView` (gap-reset + shields applied, NOT raw `playerQuestStates.streak`), the bucket "improvement"/promotion rule is defined (what makes a bucket better) along with the keep-or-re-derive-`subBucket` decision on a promotion, the `uint88 weightedBurn` overflow policy is decided (base × time-mult ≤20× × boost ≤20× ≈ 400× base — saturate or prove headroom), the double-count policy vs the burn-time `multBps` streak lever is resolved (keep both levers vs strip streak from burn-time), and the shields consume-vs-read decision is made — recorded for the IMPL (TDEC-01 is owned at IMPL; its design is fixed here).
  3. The terminal-decimator freeze-safety is RE-PROVEN under the bucket-promotion allowance (TDEC-03 SPEC half) — since TDEC-01 now allows a bucket PROMOTION (not only a within-bucket share increase), the validator's original `subBucket`-fixed simplification no longer holds, so SPEC re-proves freeze-safety on the basis "all weight + bucket mutation precedes the draw" (the boost + any promotion are DETERMINISTIC from the player's fixed effective-streak factor × their burn, committed in the same tx BEFORE `gameOver` flips and BEFORE subbuckets are drawn from `rngWord` → the player cannot use draw knowledge to manipulate placement), the `require(!gameOver)` gate + the pool-finalized-in-resolution + the shares-sum-to-pool invariants are re-attested — recorded for the IMPL (TDEC-01 builds it; the freeze-safety proof is the SPEC's design gate).
  4. The UDVT width/byte-preservation discipline is locked (UDVT-01/02/03 design feed) — the per-site decision matrix is fixed: which `abi.encodePacked(…day…)` RNG-entropy sites cast to `uint32` (`DegenerusGameAdvanceModule.sol:1828`/`:1405`, `DegenerusGame.sol:1011` — to preserve the exact keccak preimage byte-image), which packed `Sub`/struct day fields stay uint24-backed (no cold-slot spill — the v56 gas win), which standalone day slots + indexed day event topics widen to `uint32` explicitly, and the `rngWordByDay` mapping KEY is confirmed layout-unchanged (uint24/uint32 zero-pad to the same slot); the operator-overload set (`<`, `<=`, `==`, `%`, `+`, `-`) + solc 0.8.34 UDVT support is confirmed — recorded for the IMPL (UDVT-01/02/03 are owned at IMPL; their byte-preservation discipline is fixed here).
  5. The freeze/solvency re-attestation lands + every cited `file:line` is grep-attested vs `1e7a646d` (SEC design feed) — the RNG-freeze-intact (across all 8 items, the UDVT byte-image being load-bearing) + SOLVENCY-byte properties are re-attested on paper as the SPEC's design gate (5 of 6 items are BURNIE-credit / weight-only / pure-annotation OFF the ETH/`claimablePool` path; the BURNIE fix keeps the ETH/pool DEBIT byte-unchanged but RESTORES ticket claims on the pools — the posture widening is flagged) (SEC-01/02 are owned at TST; their design is fixed here); and every cited anchor across the milestone scope (the `handlePurchase`/`MintModule` fold sites, the `_resolveFullTicketBet` hook + `whalePassClaims`/`claimWhalePass`, the `DegenerusGameDecimatorModule` machinery + the `TerminalDecEntry` packing + `getPlayerQuestView`, the 3 `abi.encodePacked` sites + the day-bearing surface, the BURNIE-path `_purchaseCoinFor`/`_callTicketPurchase`/`_queueTicketsScaled`/`gamePurchaseTicketsBurnie` anchors, the stale `gameSetAutoRebuy`/`_runRewardJackpots`/3-arg-`purchaseCoin` references) is grep-verified against `1e7a646d` with any drift corrected in the SPEC (no "by construction" survives un-checked).
  6. The BURNIE coin-buy ticket-queue Critical fix is design-locked (BURNIE-03 — the SPEC design half) — the verified bug (`_purchaseCoinFor` `DegenerusGameMintModule.sol:887-907` burns the coin via `_callTicketPurchase(payInCoin=true)` but DISCARDS the returns → ZERO tickets queued; phase-160 `24f0898b` orphaned the coin path) is documented with all 4 decisive anchors, and the fix is locked: (a) BURNIE-01 — capture the returns + `_queueTicketsScaled(buyer, targetLevel, adjustedQty, false)`; (b) BURNIE-02 — the MINT_BURNIE-leg-only `handlePurchase` routing (skip score/affiliate/non-mint-quests) + the burn-REBATE mechanic (require the FULL ticket cost upfront, defer the burn, burn net = full − MINT_BURNIE reward floored at 0) co-designed with BATCH-01's return-instead-of-credit; (c) the freeze framing (`purchaseCoin` reads no `rngWord`) + the SOLVENCY posture-widening (ETH debit byte-unchanged, ticket claims restored, no unbacked obligation) — recorded for the IMPL (BURNIE-01/02 owned at 359; their design is fixed here).
  7. The sDGNRS salvage-swap combo ETH/BURNIE pawn-shop payout is design-locked (SALVAGE-02 — the SPEC design half) — the verified current structure (`sellFarFutureTickets` `DegenerusGame.sol:2074`→`MintModule.sol:929`; quote `MintStreakUtils.sol:145-190` with the prior-day `seed`, `jitterMult` 70–110%, `ticketShareBps` 40–80% → cash ≤60%; ETH relabel `MintModule:975-977`; `_ethToBurnieValue` `:1657`; `creditFlip`; `rngLockedFlag`-gated) is documented, and the change is locked: split the cash leg `cashWei` into `ethWei` (full-range `[0..ethCap]` from a NEW slice of the prior-day seed; `ethCap` = the existing eth-% cap) + a BURNIE part paid by TRANSFERRING sDGNRS-OWNED BURNIE (token balance + claimable coinflip stake), valued via `_ethToBurnieValue` @ current eth-equivalent — **NOT a `creditFlip` mint** (USER): `actualBurnie = min(target, sDGNRS-available)`, the remainder + the zero-available case paid as ETH ("do it more like now"); ticket leg unchanged. **The "pawn-shop" safety model is the SPEC's load-bearing proof:** offers are VARIABLE + KNOWABLE-IN-ADVANCE (no hidden VRF — reuses the settled prior-day word), and the SOLE non-exploitability property is the **total payout cap (the existing no-arb ceiling) + the eth-% cap** — every reachable offer ≤ the cap → no extraction above it regardless of optimization (suboptimal players forfeit EV to the protocol/pools, intended); SOLVENCY-positive (only the ETH part leaves SDGNRS; the BURNIE is sDGNRS-owned, TRANSFERRED — NO new emission; source-availability check prevents over-draw). The no-arb re-proof obligation (extend `SWAP08_NoArbAtCeiling` to the new variability + the fallback) is owned here, verified at SALVAGE-03 (TST). Grep-attest anchors vs `1e7a646d`. Recorded for the IMPL (SALVAGE-01 owned at 359).
  8. The manual-sub-cancel auto-claim + auto-evict pure-forfeit is design-locked (CANCEL-02 — the SPEC design half) — the verified latent loss bug is documented (manual cancel `GameAfkingModule:345-362` tombstones + leaves `pendingBurnie`/`affiliateBase` in the slot, but the next `processSubscriberStage` reclaim `delete _subOf[player]` `:1144` wipes both → loss in the race), and the fix is locked: manual cancel auto-claims BEFORE clearing — pay the canceller's `pendingBurnie` via `creditFlip` (+ presale-box parity, mirror `claimAfkingBurnie:1560`) + drain `affiliateBase` and settle the tree A/U1/U2 75/20/5 (mirror `DegenerusAffiliate.claim:629`/`drainAffiliateBase:1605`), then `_finalizeAfking`+clear; AUTO-EVICT (pass `:1175` / funding `:1226` / reclaim `:1144`) stays a pure FORFEIT (delete both accumulators, no payout — USER). Freeze/solvency re-attested: BURNIE-emission only (`creditFlip`), no `rngWord` read, no ETH/`claimablePool` touch, `rngLock`-gated at the `subscribe` entry, CEI (zero before credit). Grep-attest anchors vs `1e7a646d`. Recorded for the IMPL (CANCEL-01 owned at 359).

### Phase 359: IMPL — The ONE Carefully-Sequenced Batched Contract Diff (handlePurchase batching + WWXRP whale-halfpass + terminal-decimator boost + the wide UDVT refactor)

**Goal**: The v57.0 bundle lands as a single reconciled `contracts/*.sol` diff under the SPEC's settled shapes, authored producer-before-consumer (the small-feature edits → the wide UDVT refactor → interfaces/wiring): the `handlePurchase` BURNIE-flip batching (BATCH-01 return-instead-of-credit + BATCH-02 naming correction), the WWXRP jackpot whale-halfpass (WWXRP-01 per-bracket grant at `_resolveFullTicketBet`), the terminal-decimator final-day streak boost (TDEC-01 `boostTerminalDecimator()` with bucket promotion), the BURNIE coin-buy ticket-queue Critical fix (BURNIE-01 `_purchaseCoinFor` queue-on-return + BURNIE-02 MINT_BURNIE burn-rebate, co-designed with BATCH-01), and the repo-wide `type Day is uint24` UDVT (UDVT-01 the type + overloads, UDVT-02 the `abi.encodePacked` uint32 casts, UDVT-03 the storage-layout/gas preservation) — the wide UDVT refactor DOMINATES this phase. Applied to `contracts/` and locally compiling (`forge build` clean), then HELD at the contract-commit boundary for explicit user hand-review.
**Type**: IMPL (CONTRACT BOUNDARY — the ONE carefully-sequenced batched USER-APPROVED `contracts/*.sol` diff; `autonomous: false` at the commit gate; never auto-commit contracts)
**Depends on**: Phase 358 (the SPEC must lock the WWXRP rationing key + recipient policy, the terminal-decimator design decisions + the bucket-promotion freeze re-proof, the UDVT per-site cast/keep/widen discipline, the BURNIE queue-on-return + burn-rebate design, and grep-attest the edit-order first)
**Requirements**: BATCH-01, BATCH-02, WWXRP-01, TDEC-01, UDVT-01, UDVT-02, UDVT-03, BURNIE-01, BURNIE-02, SALVAGE-01, CANCEL-01
**Success Criteria** (what must be TRUE):

  1.   2. The WWXRP jackpot whale-halfpass lands rationed per bracket (WWXRP-01) — a player who hits the Degenerette jackpot (`s == 9`) on a `currency == CURRENCY_WWXRP` (=3) bet with `amountPerTicket >= MIN_BET_WWXRP` is awarded a Whale halfpass via `whalePassClaims[player] += 1`, RATIONED to one award per 10-level bracket (a per-bracket award flag keyed by `level/10` — NOT a global 0→5 lifetime cap), hooked at `DegeneretteModule._resolveFullTicketBet` (~:713, after the s≥7 sDGNRS award), with the new `wwxrpJackpotWhalePass*` per-bracket state in `DegenerusGameStorage`, the recipient + multi-bracket policy from SPEC applied, reusing the `claimWhalePass` future-ticket deferral (no ETH/`claimablePool` touch), and short-circuiting to zero added cost on non-jackpot spins.
  3. The terminal-decimator final-day streak boost lands with bucket promotion (TDEC-01) — a new `boostTerminalDecimator()` lets a player on the final day multiply their `weightedBurn` by their effective quest-streak factor (validated via `getPlayerQuestView` — the EFFECTIVE streak with gap-reset + shields, NOT raw `playerQuestStates.streak`; streak 100→20×, 10→4×) folded into `terminalDecBucketBurnTotal[key]` via the existing `keccak256(abi.encode(lvl,bucket,subBucket))` key, with a `boosted` bit added to the packed `TerminalDecEntry` for idempotence, AND PROMOTES the player's bucket if the boosted weight qualifies for an improved bucket (per the SPEC improvement + keep-vs-re-derive-subBucket rule), overflow-handled per the SPEC `uint88` policy, reusing the live `DegenerusGameDecimatorModule` machinery (`recordTerminalDecBurn`/`runTerminalDecimatorJackpot`/`_terminalDecMultiplierBps`), gated by `require(!gameOver)`, landing same-tx before `gameOver` flips and before subbuckets are drawn (the freeze-safety carried as an IMPL invariant, re-proven at TST).
  4. The repo-wide `type Day is uint24` UDVT lands byte-preserving + layout-preserving (UDVT-01 / UDVT-02 / UDVT-03 — the heavy item) — the `type Day is uint24` value type + global operator overloads (`<`, `<=`, `==`, `%`, `+`, `-`) replace the raw day-counter integers across the ~649-line/27-contract day-bearing surface with zero behavior change (UDVT-01); the RNG byte-image is preserved bit-for-bit — every `abi.encodePacked(…day…)` RNG-entropy site explicitly casts the day to `uint32` (`DegenerusGameAdvanceModule.sol:1828`/`:1405`, `DegenerusGame.sol:1011` — an unwrapped uint24-backed `Day` would shorten the keccak preimage and change the derived word), the `rngWordByDay` mapping KEY layout unchanged (UDVT-02); and storage layout + gas are preserved — packed `Sub`/struct day fields stay uint24-backed (no cold-slot spill → the v56 gas win intact), standalone day slots + indexed day event topics widen to `uint32` explicitly (UDVT-03).
  5. The diff is producer-before-consumer + `forge build` is clean + HELD at the boundary (all 9 IMPL reqs) — the whole diff is authored producer-before-consumer per the SPEC edit-order map (small-feature edits → the BURNIE coin-buy fix → the wide UDVT refactor → interfaces/wiring), applied to `contracts/` and locally compiling (`forge build` clean; `ContractAddresses.sol` freely modifiable), but NOT committed without explicit user hand-review of the single batched diff (the SOLVENCY ETH/`claimablePool` DEBIT path stays byte-unchanged across all items — the BURNIE fix restores ticket claims without an unbacked obligation — and RNG-freeze stays intact via the UDVT uint32 casts, both carried as IMPL invariants and re-proven at TST 361).

RNG-freeze unaffected (`purchaseCoin` reads no `rngWord`); ETH/pool DEBIT byte-unchanged (restored ticket claims create no unbacked obligation), both re-proven at TST 361.
  7. Only the ETH part is relabeled out of `claimableWinnings[SDGNRS]` (NO new BURNIE emission) → solvency-positive. Every reachable offer stays ≤ the no-arb ceiling + the eth-% cap (the pawn-shop safety invariant, re-proven at TST 361 / SALVAGE-03).

BURNIE-emission only (no `rngWord`, no ETH/`claimablePool` touch), `rngLock`-gated at the subscribe entry; SOLVENCY-untouched + RNG-freeze-clean, re-proven at TST 361 / CANCEL-03.

**Center-of-gravity rationale (where a requirement spans design + impl + test + close):**

- **WWXRP-02** (the design half — the per-bracket rationing key + the operator-recipient policy + the multi-bracket-allow decision) → SPEC (358), where the rationing-key + recipient decisions are LOCKED BEFORE any code (they are design choices, not built behaviors). **WWXRP-01** (the BUILT per-bracket grant at `_resolveFullTicketBet`) → IMPL (359). No double-counting: WWXRP-02 = the design rule the IMPL applies; WWXRP-01 = the grant the IMPL builds.
- **TDEC-02 / TDEC-03** (the design half — the effective-streak source / bucket-improvement + promotion rule / `uint88` overflow / double-count / shields decisions [TDEC-02], and the freeze-safety RE-PROOF under the bucket-promotion allowance [TDEC-03]) → SPEC (358), where they are settled on paper BEFORE the code (the bucket-promotion freeze re-proof is load-bearing — TDEC-01 now allows promotion, so the validator's original `subBucket`-fixed simplification no longer holds). **TDEC-01** (the BUILT `boostTerminalDecimator()` + bucket promotion) → IMPL (359). No double-counting.

The UDVT byte-preservation discipline (the per-site cast/keep/widen matrix — the SPEC's SC4) is the design input folded into 358, NOT double-counted; only the requirement's HOME (where it is BUILT) is counted at IMPL.
- **GAS phase (360) owns NO REQ-ID** — it is the gas-neutrality measurement gate. UDVT-03 ("storage layout + gas preserved + NON-WIDENING") is OWNED at IMPL (where the uint24-keep/uint32-widen discipline is BUILT); its gas-neutrality half is MEASURED at GAS (the packed Sub day fields stay uint24 / no cold-slot spill), and its NON-WIDENING-regression half is PROVEN at TST. The GAS phase exists because the UDVT must be PROVEN gas-neutral (the v56 packed-Sub gas win is load-bearing) — a measurement gate, not a requirement owner. (Unlike v55/v56, whose GAS phases owned GAS-* requirements, v57 has no GAS-* requirements — the bundle is gas-neutral-by-construction, so the GAS phase records Outcome-A no-diff in the expected case.)
- **SEC-01 / SEC-02 · HYG-01 / HYG-02** → TST (361). SEC-01/02 (RNG-freeze intact incl. the UDVT per-site byte-diff gate + SOLVENCY-01 byte-untouched) are PROVEN empirically as the hard gate (the SPEC re-attestation at 358's SC5 is the design gate, NOT a separate count); the TERMINAL adversarial review (AUDIT-01) re-confirms SEC, but SEC-01/02's center-of-gravity (where the property is first PROVEN) is TST. HYG-01/02 (the test/comment hygiene) land here because they are test-file + comment edits — no contract logic change, so they do NOT belong in the IMPL contract diff; they ride the TST phase (AGENT-committable, no contract-commit gate).

## ✅ v56.0 AfKing Everyday-Gas Minimization (SHIPPED 2026-06-04 — closure signal `MILESTONE_V56_AT_HEAD_1e7a646d44da4ee26375edd0b006274821fef73e`; subject frozen `1e7a646d`; baseline `453f8073`; 0 NEW_FINDINGS; THE FIRST TERMINAL to mutate contracts/ across SIX gates)

**Milestone:** v56.0 (started 2026-06-01)
**Defined:** 2026-06-01
**Audit baseline → subject:** v55.0 closure HEAD — frozen contract subject `453f8073`, closure signal `MILESTONE_V55_AT_HEAD_ca3bbd3220de763298ef2e742111f6e6ef90d583` → v56.0 closure HEAD. Subject = the single carefully-sequenced batched `contracts/*.sol` diff for the mode-agnostic aggregator + the ticket-mode minimal-write primitive + the open-end optimizations + the shared-`DegenerusQuests`-core batched-settle entrypoint. Every cited `file:line` MUST be re-attested against the v55.0-closure HEAD `453f8073` before any patch.
**Scope source:** `.planning/REQUIREMENTS.md` (24 v56.0 REQ-IDs across 8 categories: AGG 5 · TKT 2 · AFF 2 · QST 5 · OPEN 2 · GAS 4 · SEC 2 · XMODEL 1 · AUDIT 1) + the milestone init (2026-06-01) + the design-lock input `.planning/PLAN-V56-AFKING-BATCHING-GAS.md` + the `[[v56-batch-afking-affiliate-quest-seed]]` memory. **No research** — a fully-specced internal contract gas+batching refactor with a USER-converged mechanism (the mode-agnostic ~10-day aggregator); the design explorations (affiliate-distribution non-gameability, ticket-mode parity) are resolved in the plan doc.

> **Scope (USER-locked):** the AFKING SYSTEM specifically — **BOTH ENDS: the BUYING (the per-day process STAGE / accrual / settle) AND the OPENING (the box open-pass / materialize).** Make the whole afking path maximally gas-efficient while remaining COMPLETELY secure and UNMANIPULABLE (no economic edge from any "fuckery" — with PARTICULAR focus on gaining an edge by subscribing/unsubscribing strategically). NOT a whole-ecosystem sweep — afking buy + open only (shared-code touches handled with care).

> **Posture — NOT a behavior-identical pass.** Slight semantic simplifications are acceptable if they cut gas and stay unmanipulable; the hard floor is unmanipulable + secure (enforced by a mandatory 3-skill adversarial economic review PLUS a baked-in cross-model Codex + Gemini review — XMODEL-01). The unifying design (USER-converged 2026-06-01) is a MODE-AGNOSTIC accrue-cheap-per-buy aggregator that settles all affiliate + quest ("the extraneous stuff") for BOTH ticket and lootbox subs: accrue cheap per-buy into a per-sub accumulator (NO cross-contract calls), then settle per-leg — the AFFILIATE leg is a flat-7% deterministic-split PULL (`claim`/`withdraw`, NO scheduled flush, NO roll) and the QUEST leg settles AUTOMATICALLY by RIDING THE DAILY BUY STAGE on the global settle day (`currentDay % settlePeriod == 0`, ~10-day cadence — the slot-0 `questProgress` delivered-day counter mints `× QUEST_SLOT0_REWARD` **+ the accrued `buyerOwedBurnie` 10%/20% ticket buyer-bonus** in ONE `creditFlip` to the sub) + a permissionless `claimQuest(subs[])` keeper-liveness fallback (+ quest-settle-on-unsub) — _amended 2026-06-01 — quest settle RIDES THE BUY STAGE (the separate `mintBurnie` "settlement-due" router leg is REJECTED as a redundant cold-SLOAD pass; `SUB_STAGE_BATCH` SHRUNK so the settle-day chunk fits 16.7M, number deferred to 355); the afking ticket buyer-bonus 10%/20% is accrued + settled with the quest (matches live `:1655`); first-sub-only +daysToNextSettle streak, no provisional: SUPERSEDES the prior "scheduled-roll/player-flush-replays-the-roll" mechanism; the roll is removed_. Each mode's per-day work collapses to a minimal primitive — lootbox = the existing box-stamp; ticket = a NEW custom "write the ticket entries to the queue" fn that mirrors the box-stamp (dropping the per-day `MintModule.purchaseWith` ~262k heavyweight, **but ACCRUING the 10%/20% ticket buyer-bonus `:1655-1659` into `buyerOwedBurnie` at live parity — closing the v55-style dropped-bonus regression**). Plus a STAGE gas sweep (accumulator in the `Sub` slot's spare bits, `SUB_STAGE_BATCH` re-tune, mode/SLOAD collapse) + fold-in O1 (the pre-existing `DegenerusQuests` lootbox-quest BURNIE double-credit, surfaced at the v55 close).

> **Why it is unexploitable (the load-bearing non-exploitability fact, carried into SEC/XMODEL):** the afking affiliate distribution is a **flat-7% deterministic-split PULL** with NO roll and NO seed (_amended 2026-06-01 — flat-7% deterministic-split pull; quests stay automatic: SUPERSEDES the prior daily-seeded roll_) — per buy accrue a flat `_ethToBurnie(eth)×7/100` into the running `affiliateBase`, settle by PULL via `claim` with the fixed 75/20/5 split + `withdraw` (CEI). The **buyer never receives the base** (`A ≠ sub` guaranteed + the rare U1/U2==sub cycle skip, `DegenerusAffiliate.sol:579`) → no settle-timing profit. Because there is exactly ONE deterministic distribution path (no roll, no seed, no scheduled-vs-player-flush divergence), there is **no favorable seed to select AND no two-distribution free option to arbitrage** — the XMODEL C1/C2 free-option finding is MOOT (the roll is removed). The taper is afking-N/A (flat 7%; the anti-concentration taper applies to manual buys only). No double-settle: self-marking running balances (`affiliateBase` zeroed at `claim`; the slot-0 `questProgress` delivered-day counter drained at the automatic `mintBurnie` settlement-due flush — or the permissionless `claimQuest(subs[])` fallback) — the per-sub `windowStartDay`/`lastSettledDay` markers are DROPPED. Streak-farming is gated by the active-pass check + the `lastCompletedDay`/`afkCoveredThroughDay` double-credit guards + the per-window streak advancing only on debit-DELIVERED days; the first-sub-only `+daysToNextSettle` head-start is bounded +0..+9 once/account (USER-ACCEPTED-BY-DESIGN — the bound replaces the prior confirmed-vs-provisional escrow; sybil farming is pass-cost-gated — _amended 2026-06-01 — automatic slot-0 BURNIE via mintBurnie chain + claimQuest fallback; first-sub-only +daysToNextSettle streak, no provisional_). Adversarially re-cleared (economic-analyst + zero-day-hunter, no Medium+).

> **Cross-cutting rule (every requirement):** every cited `file:line` MUST be re-attested against the **v55.0 closure HEAD `453f8073`** before any patch (no "by construction" / "single fn reaches all paths" claim survives un-checked — the `DegenerusGame` mint/jackpot inline-duplication precedent; `feedback_verify_call_graph_against_source`). The cited anchors (the per-buy cross-contract storm `GameAfkingModule.sol:760-831` / the lootbox stamp branch `:735-749` / the ticket-mode `purchaseWith` route `:713-731`; the affiliate daily-seeded roll `DegenerusAffiliate.sol:558`/`:579` + the leaderboard `affiliateCoinEarned[lvl]` + `_updateTopAffiliate`; the `DegenerusQuests.handlePurchase` double-credit `:890` + `awardQuestStreakBonus`; the afking open path `_openAfkingBox`→`resolveAfkingBox` + `mintBurnie`/`autoOpen`/`OPEN_BATCH`; the `Sub` 4-field stamp `(scorePlus1, amount, lastAutoBoughtDay)` + `lastOpenedDay` in `DegenerusGameStorage`; the `_applyEvMultiplierWithCap`/`lootboxEvBenefitUsedByLevel[player][level+1]` EV-cap; the STAGE placement in `DegenerusGameAdvanceModule`) are confirmed at SPEC. **Security / freeze / solvency floor over gas** (`feedback_security_over_gas`): SEC-01 (unmanipulable, esp. strategic sub/unsub) + SEC-02 (SOLVENCY-01 untouched — affiliate/quest stay BURNIE flip-credit OFF the ETH/`claimablePool` path; RNG-freeze intact) are the hard gate. Pre-launch redeploy-fresh (storage-layout break fine, no migration; `feedback_frozen_contracts_no_future_proofing`).

> **Posture:** the contract changes ship as ONE carefully-sequenced batched USER-APPROVED `contracts/*.sol` diff with a **HARD STOP at the contract-commit boundary** (applied + locally compiled/tested, NEVER committed without explicit user hand-review — `feedback_batch_contract_approval` + `feedback_never_preapprove_contracts` + `feedback_manual_review_before_push` + `feedback_no_contract_commits`; `ContractAddresses.sol` freely modifiable per `feedback_contractaddresses_policy`). (completed 2026-06-01)

## Phase Details

### Phase 353: SPEC — Design-Lock + Unmanipulable/Solvency Re-Attestation + XMODEL Design-Input + Call-Graph Attestation

**Goal**: The v56.0 mechanism is settled in writing so the IMPL phase authors a fully reconciled diff with zero "by construction" assumptions, and the load-bearing non-exploitability + non-perturbation are designed BEFORE any code is written: the mode-agnostic ~10-day aggregator (the affiliate accrue/settle split + the per-sub accumulator storage layout + the double-settle markers), the ticket-mode minimal-write primitive shape (+ the century/x00 parity decision), the afking-OPEN-end review (the materialization + the unmanipulable re-verification), the shared-`DegenerusQuests`-core batched-settle entrypoint shape + the non-perturbation approach, and the QST design (automatic slot-0 BURNIE via the `mintBurnie` settlement-due chain + a `claimQuest` fallback; the first-sub-only `+daysToNextSettle` streak head-start [bounded +0..+9, no provisional] — _amended 2026-06-01 — automatic slot-0 BURNIE via mintBurnie chain + claimQuest fallback; first-sub-only +daysToNextSettle streak, no provisional_) are LOCKED; the unmanipulable (esp. strategic sub/unsub) + SOLVENCY-01-untouched + RNG-freeze-intact properties are re-attested on paper; the XMODEL-01 cross-model design-input pass (Codex + Gemini crafted prompts) is run and its gas suggestions + exploit findings folded into the design-lock BEFORE IMPL; and every cited `file:line` is grep-verified against the v55.0 HEAD `453f8073` — paper-only, zero `contracts/*.sol`.
**Type**: SPEC
**Depends on**: Nothing (first v56.0 phase; consumes the v55.0 closure HEAD `453f8073` as the frozen audit baseline, plus the design-lock input `.planning/PLAN-V56-AFKING-BATCHING-GAS.md` + the `[[v56-batch-afking-affiliate-quest-seed]]` memory)
**Requirements**: AFF-01, AFF-02, XMODEL-01
**Success Criteria** (what must be TRUE):

  1. The affiliate distribution is design-locked + proven non-gameable (AFF-01 / AFF-02) — the afking affiliate distribution is a **flat-7% deterministic-split PULL**: accrue `_ethToBurnie(ethSpent)×7/100` (flat, no taper, no kickback) per buy into the sub's running `affiliateBase`; settle by PULL via `claim(address[] subs)` (same-affiliate batch, ONE `sumB`, the fixed 75/20/5 split computed once → `pendingClaim[A/U1/U2]`, buyer-never-wins via `A ≠ sub` guaranteed + the rare U1/U2==sub cycle skip); `withdraw()` = the only cross-contract `creditFlip` (CEI). There is NO roll, NO seed, NO scheduled/mutation affiliate flush — so settle-timing can NEVER select a favorable seed AND no two-distribution free option can exist (exactly ONE deterministic path) (amended 2026-06-01 — flat-7% deterministic-split pull; quests stay automatic: SUPERSEDES the XMODEL roll-unification — the roll itself is REMOVED, so the C1/C2 free-option finding is MOOT; adversarially re-cleared, economic-analyst + zero-day-hunter, no Medium+) (the load-bearing non-exploitability fact: the split is EV-neutral + intra-upline-chain-only-redistributive + buyer-never-wins, `DegenerusAffiliate.sol:579`, re-attested) (AFF-01); the activity taper is afking-N/A (flat 7%; `_applyLootboxTaper` applies to MANUAL buys only), and the affiliate leaderboard credits at `claim` time to the direct affiliate `A` (USER-accepted claim-time distortion — there is no scheduled affiliate settle under the pull) (AFF-02).

  2. The mode-agnostic aggregator + the per-sub accumulator storage layout + the self-marking settle are design-locked (AFF-01/AFF-02 inputs; AGG/GAS-02 design feed) — the affiliate leg is PULL (no scheduled flush) while the QUEST leg settles uniformly for BOTH ticket and lootbox subs (the single mode-agnostic quest-settle path); the per-sub accumulator layout is decided (the SHRUNK in-slot `affiliateBase uint32 (whole-BURNIE, 100M clamp)` + `questProgress` running balances re-packed into the same Sub slot — attested at 232/256, NOT the stale "176/256" premise — plus the off-slot `pendingClaim` mapping for the affiliate recipients); and double-settle is impossible via **self-marking running balances** — the affiliate `claim` zeroes `affiliateBase[sub]` and the quest flush drains `questProgress` (both a no-op on a double-fire), so the per-sub `windowStartDay`/`lastSettledDay`/`settledThroughDay` markers are DROPPED — recorded for the IMPL to BUILD (amended 2026-06-01 — flat-7% deterministic-split pull; quests stay automatic) (AGG-01..05 / GAS-02 are owned at IMPL/GAS; their design is fixed here).

  3. The ticket-mode minimal-write primitive + the afking-OPEN-end review are design-locked (TKT/OPEN design feed) — the custom "write the ticket entries to the queue" fn shape is locked (a cheap `_queueTicketsScaled`-equivalent primitive mirroring the lootbox box-stamp, producing resolution-equivalent placement/trait/quantity, the affiliate + quest deferred to the aggregator), and the afking-ticket century/x00 quantity-bonus parity (`MintModule:1243`) keep-or-drop decision is made (allowed to drop for simplicity under the scope latitude); and the afking-OPEN-end (`_openAfkingBox`→`resolveAfkingBox` + `mintBurnie`/`autoOpen`/`OPEN_BATCH`) is reviewed for the cheapest viable materialization shared with the human path AND re-verified unmanipulable (live-level parity, no double-open, no EV-cap double-draw, no shared-state hazard) — recorded for the IMPL (TKT-01/02 + OPEN-01/02 are owned at IMPL; their design is fixed here).

  4. The shared-`DegenerusQuests`-core non-perturbation approach + the QST design (automatic slot-0 BURNIE + first-sub-only streak head-start) are design-locked + the O1 disposition is decided (QST design feed; amended 2026-06-01 — automatic slot-0 BURNIE via mintBurnie chain + claimQuest fallback; first-sub-only +daysToNextSettle streak, no provisional) — the batched-settle entrypoint added to the shared `DegenerusQuests` core has a locked shape with a non-perturbation approach (PROVE non-perturbing to the manual / bingo / degenerette / boon callers — `awardQuestStreakBonus` etc.); the QST settle/streak design is derived — slot-0 completion accrues a delivered-day `questProgress` COUNTER → settled = mint `× QUEST_SLOT0_REWARD` via the `mintBurnie` "settlement-due" router chain when due (~10-day cadence) + a permissionless `claimQuest(subs[])` keeper-liveness fallback (always credits the sub, never the caller) + a quest-settle-on-unsub (slot-1 stays MANUAL; the ±10 streak is the activity-score multiplier, NOT direct BURNIE), the streak uses a SIMPLIFIED first-sub-only `+daysToNextSettle` head-start (`hasEverSubscribed` 1-bit; bounded +0..+9 over the manual baseline, no provisional/vesting) on the ±10-per-window model (−10 on unsub) with the per-window streak advancing only on debit-DELIVERED days, the `lastCompletedDay`/`afkCoveredThroughDay` double-credit guard + active-pass anti-reset (slot rewards NEVER suppressed); the bounded +0..+9 first-sub head-start is USER-ACCEPTED-BY-DESIGN (the bound REPLACES the prior confirmed-vs-provisional escrow for the afking grant — a deliberate accepted tradeoff, NOT a missed control; the activity-score still reads the actual `state.streak`); and the pre-existing O1 lootbox-quest BURNIE double-credit (`DegenerusQuests.handlePurchase` internal `creditFlip` + the returned-and-re-credited value, `:890`) is adjudicated intended-vs-bug with the fix designed if a genuine over-mint — recorded for the IMPL (QST-01..05 are owned at IMPL; their design is fixed here).

  5. The unmanipulable/solvency/freeze re-attestation + the XMODEL design-input pass land + every cited `file:line` is grep-attested vs `453f8073` (XMODEL-01; SEC design feed) — the unmanipulable property (esp. the strategic sub/unsub edge), SOLVENCY-01-untouched (the affiliate/quest stay BURNIE flip-credit OFF the ETH/`claimablePool` path; this is a BURNIE-emission-timing change only), and RNG-freeze-intact-under-the-new-accrual/settle are re-attested on paper as the SPEC's design gate (SEC-01/02 are owned at TST; their design is fixed here); the XMODEL-01 cross-model DESIGN-INPUT pass is run — Codex + Gemini are fed crafted prompts covering the FULL afking system (the BUYING STAGE/accrual/settle AND the OPENING open-pass/materialize) for (a) long-run gas-optimization suggestions and (b) adversarial verification that the design is completely unmanipulable (PARTICULAR focus on the strategic sub/unsub edge), and the suggestions + exploit findings are folded into the design-lock BEFORE IMPL (this is XMODEL-01's primary deliverable / home; its TERMINAL close-augmentation half is reflected in Phase 357's success criteria); and every cited anchor across the milestone scope (the per-buy cross-contract storm + the lootbox stamp branch + the ticket `purchaseWith` route in `GameAfkingModule`, the affiliate roll + leaderboard sites, the `DegenerusQuests.handlePurchase` double-credit + `awardQuestStreakBonus`, the afking open path, the `Sub` stamp + the EV-cap map, the STAGE placement in `DegenerusGameAdvanceModule`) is grep-verified against `453f8073` with any drift corrected in the SPEC (no "by construction" survives un-checked).

**Plans**: 2 plans (Wave 1: 353-01 SPEC core authoring [AFF-01/AFF-02 + AGG/TKT/QST/OPEN design feeds + corrected accumulator slot + anchor attestation + threat-model re-attestation]; Wave 2: 353-02 XMODEL-01 cross-model design-input pass [codex + gemini × 5 concerns] + disposition fold-in + SPEC lock)

### Phase 354: IMPL — The ONE Carefully-Sequenced Batched Contract Diff (aggregator + ticket-mode primitive + DegenerusQuests batched-settle + accumulator + open-end)

**Goal**: The v56.0 mechanism lands as a single reconciled `contracts/*.sol` diff under the SPEC's settled shapes, authored producer-before-consumer (accumulator storage → the aggregator accrue/settle in the STAGE → the `DegenerusQuests` batched-settle entrypoint → the ticket-mode minimal-write primitive → the open-end optimizations → the interface/wiring): the per-sub accumulator appended/packed into `DegenerusGameStorage`; the inline `_settleQuest` mints `questProgress × QUEST_SLOT0_REWARD` + `buyerOwedBurnie` in ONE `creditFlip`; `SUB_STAGE_BATCH` SHRUNK so the settle-day chunk fits 16.7M, deferred to 355] + a quest-settle-on-unsub + the uniform mode-agnostic quest-settle for BOTH ticket + lootbox subs + the self-marking running balances [`windowStartDay`/`lastSettledDay` double-settle markers DROPPED]); the ticket-mode minimal-write primitive (the custom "write the ticket entries to the queue" fn replacing the per-day `purchaseWith` heavyweight, the inline affiliate/quest deferred to the aggregator, producing resolution-equivalent ticket entries with the century/x00 parity decision applied + ACCRUING the 10%/20% ticket buyer-bonus `:1655-1659` into `buyerOwedBurnie` at live parity [closing the v55-style dropped-bonus regression]); the `DegenerusQuests` batched-settle entrypoint + the streak machinery (amended 2026-06-01 — quest settle rides the buy STAGE; slot-0 BURNIE + the 10%/20% ticket buyer-bonus mint together; first-sub-only +daysToNextSettle streak, no provisional) (the slot-0 `questProgress` delivered-day counter → settle-mint `× QUEST_SLOT0_REWARD` [+ the accrued `buyerOwedBurnie` ticket bonus] via the STAGE-riding settle on the global settle day / `claimQuest` fallback, the first-sub-only `+daysToNextSettle` head-start [bounded +0..+9, no provisional] with the activity-score reading the actual `state.streak` and the per-window streak advancing only on debit-DELIVERED days, the `lastCompletedDay`/`afkCoveredThroughDay` double-credit guard + active-pass anti-reset with slot rewards never suppressed, proven non-perturbing to the manual/bingo/degenerette/boon callers, and the O1 lootbox-quest double-credit confirmed-intended-or-fixed); and the open-end optimizations (the `_openAfkingBox`→`resolveAfkingBox` + `mintBurnie`/`autoOpen`/`OPEN_BATCH` path optimized for max gas with the cheapest viable shared materialization + no cold ledger, the open kept COMPLETELY unmanipulable — live-level parity, no double-open via `lastOpenedDay` monotone, no EV-cap double-draw on the shared `(player,level)` budget, no shared-mutable-state hazard with the human route) — applied to `contracts/` and locally compiling (`forge build` clean), then HELD at the contract-commit boundary for explicit user hand-review.
**Type**: IMPL (CONTRACT BOUNDARY — the ONE carefully-sequenced batched USER-APPROVED `contracts/*.sol` diff; `autonomous: false` at the commit gate; never auto-commit contracts)
**Depends on**: Phase 353 (the SPEC must lock the aggregator + the accumulator layout + the affiliate accrue/settle split + the ticket-mode primitive shape + the `DegenerusQuests` batched-settle entrypoint + the non-perturbation approach + the ±10-streak derivation + the open-end review + the unmanipulable/solvency re-attestation, fold in the XMODEL design-input suggestions, and grep-attest the edit-order first)
**Requirements**: AGG-01, AGG-02, AGG-03, AGG-04, AGG-05, TKT-01, TKT-02, QST-01, QST-02, QST-03, QST-04, QST-05, OPEN-01, OPEN-02
**Success Criteria** (what must be TRUE):

  1. The mode-agnostic aggregator accrues cheap + settles per-leg (AGG-01 / AGG-02 / AGG-03 / AGG-04 / AGG-05 — amended 2026-06-01 — flat-7% deterministic-split pull; quests stay automatic) — per buy the STAGE accrues the flat-7% affiliate base + quest progress (+ the `buyerOwedBurnie` 10%/20% ticket buyer-bonus on ticket subs) into the per-sub accumulator running balances with NO cross-contract calls (the cheap hot path, replacing the per-buy `handlePurchase`/`payAffiliate`/`creditFlip` storm) (AGG-01); the AFFILIATE leg is PULL (no scheduled flush) — the accrued `affiliateBase` persists for the uplines to settle via `claim`/`withdraw` (the fixed 75/20/5 split, no roll, no seed) — while AGG-02 SURVIVES carrying the QUEST leg only: the quest settle RIDES THE DAILY BUY STAGE on the global settle day (`currentDay % settlePeriod == 0`, ~10-day cadence — amended 2026-06-01: the separate `mintBurnie` "settlement-due" router leg is REJECTED as a redundant cold-SLOAD pass; the inline `_settleQuest` mints the sub's accrued quest BURNIE `questProgress × QUEST_SLOT0_REWARD` + the accrued `buyerOwedBurnie` ticket bonus in ONE `creditFlip` + applies the ±10 streak, draining both counters once per epoch; `SUB_STAGE_BATCH` SHRUNK so the settle-day chunk fits 16.7M, number deferred to 355) (quests stay AUTOMATIC — the sub's own reward) (AGG-02); any player-triggered sub mutation that ends the sub (unsub) triggers a lightweight QUEST-settle draining `questProgress` BEFORE applying the change — the affiliate base is NOT flushed on mutation, it persists for the uplines to PULL (an unsub does not forfeit the uplines' accrued affiliate) (AGG-03); the QUEST-settle path settles uniformly for BOTH ticket + lootbox subs (mode-agnostic — `questProgress` mode-independent; the affiliate base is likewise mode-agnostic and pulled uniformly via `claim`) (AGG-04); and double-settle is impossible via self-marking running balances — the affiliate `claim` zeroes `affiliateBase[sub]` and the quest flush drains `questProgress` (both a no-op on a double-fire), so the per-sub `windowStartDay`/`lastSettledDay` double-settle markers are DROPPED (AGG-05).

  2. The ticket-mode minimal-write primitive lands at parity (TKT-01 / TKT-02 — amended 2026-06-01 — the primitive accrues the 10%/20% ticket buyer-bonus, settled with the quest) — afking ticket subs use a custom minimal function that writes the ticket entries to the queue (mirrors the lootbox box-stamp) AND ACCRUES the 10%/20% ticket buyer-bonus (`DegenerusGameMintModule.sol:1655-1659` — flat 10% of the BURNIE-equivalent ticket spend, doubling to 20% for ≥10-ticket buys) into the per-sub `buyerOwedBurnie` field, and the per-day `MintModule.purchaseWith` heavyweight + its inline affiliate/quest are removed from the per-buy path (deferred to the AGG aggregator) — closing the v55-style regression where the bypass-`_callTicketPurchase` primitive silently DROPPED the buyer-bonus (TKT-01); the custom ticket-write produces the same queued ticket entries as `purchaseWith`'s ticket leg (resolution-equivalent placement/trait/quantity), the afking-ticket century / x00 quantity-bonus parity (`MintModule:1243`) keep-or-drop decision from the SPEC is applied, and the 10%/20% buyer-bonus is at PARITY with live (minus the affiliate-kickback leg), minted to the sub TOGETHER WITH the slot-0 quest reward at the quest STAGE settle [one `creditFlip`], ticket-mode-specific (lootbox subs use the boon) and riding the quest PUSH not the affiliate PULL (TKT-02).

  3. The quest batching lands non-perturbing with no pre-credit-EV inflation + no double-credit (QST-01 / QST-02 / QST-03 / QST-04 / QST-05 — amended 2026-06-01 — automatic slot-0 BURNIE via mintBurnie chain + claimQuest fallback; first-sub-only +daysToNextSettle streak, no provisional) — the afking quest streak uses a SIMPLIFIED first-sub-only `+daysToNextSettle` head-start (`hasEverSubscribed` 1-bit; bounded +0..+9 over the manual baseline, no provisional/vesting) on the ±10-per-window activity model (−10 on unsub), the slot-0 reward accrues as a delivered-day `questProgress` COUNTER → settled = mint `× QUEST_SLOT0_REWARD` (the ONLY direct quest BURNIE) via the `mintBurnie` settlement-due chain + the `claimQuest(subs[])` fallback + quest-settle-on-unsub, slot-1 remains the player's own manual quest, the ±10 streak is the activity-score multiplier NOT direct BURNIE (QST-01); the first-sub-only `+daysToNextSettle` head-start is a bounded (+0..+9, once/account) DIRECT streak grant that is USER-ACCEPTED-BY-DESIGN — the prior "read confirmed-delivered, never the +10 pre-credit" escrow guard is SIMPLIFIED AWAY for the afking grant (the bound REPLACES the escrow; a deliberate accepted tradeoff, NOT a missed control), the activity-score still reads the actual `state.streak`, and the per-window streak still advances only on debit-DELIVERED days (the C3-a streak-dodge fix stays in force) (QST-02); the afk+manual double-credit guard (`lastCompletedDay`/`afkCoveredThroughDay`) prevents double streak credit on afk-covered days, the gap-reset is suppressed via an active-pass check (anti-reset without daily writes), and slot rewards are NEVER suppressed (only the duplicate streak credit) (QST-03); the batched-settle entrypoint added to the shared `DegenerusQuests` core is non-perturbing to the manual / bingo / degenerette / boon callers (`awardQuestStreakBonus` etc.) (QST-04); and the pre-existing O1 lootbox-quest BURNIE double-credit (`handlePurchase` internal `creditFlip` + the returned-and-re-credited value) is confirmed intended or fixed (QST-05).

  4. The afking open-end is optimized + stays completely unmanipulable (OPEN-01 / OPEN-02) — the afking open path (`_openAfkingBox` → `resolveAfkingBox` + the `mintBurnie` open leg / the `autoOpen` cursor + `OPEN_BATCH`) is optimized for maximum gas efficiency (the per-open marginal + the batch cost), reading no cold ledger and sharing the cheapest viable materialization with the human path (OPEN-01); and the afking open stays COMPLETELY unmanipulable under the v56 changes — the live-level open = parity with human `openLootBox` (open is permissionless + bounty-driven, never player-timed → no tier-timing edge), no double-open (`lastOpenedDay` monotone), no EV-cap double-draw (the shared per-`(player,level)` budget), no shared-mutable-state hazard with the human route — ALL re-verified after the accrual/settle refactor (OPEN-02).

  5. The diff is producer-before-consumer + `forge build` is clean + HELD at the boundary (all 14 IMPL reqs) — the whole diff is authored producer-before-consumer per the SPEC edit-order map (accumulator storage → aggregator accrue/settle → `DegenerusQuests` batched-settle → ticket-mode primitive → open-end → interfaces/wiring), applied to `contracts/` and locally compiling (`forge build` clean; `ContractAddresses.sol` freely modifiable), but NOT committed without explicit user hand-review of the single batched diff (the SOLVENCY-01 ETH/`claimablePool` path stays byte-unchanged — affiliate/quest are BURNIE flip-credit only — and RNG-freeze stays intact, both carried as IMPL invariants and re-proven at TST 356).

### Phase 355: GAS — Measure + Tune (per-buy / per-open / per-settle marginals + accumulator packing + SUB_STAGE_BATCH re-tune + mode/SLOAD collapse)

Any net contract change rides the batched USER-APPROVED diff held at the contract-commit boundary; if the savings are structural to the IMPL refactor (the v55 Outcome-A precedent), that is recorded as the outcome.

The harness measures the `creditFlip` component cost so the post-swap settle marginal + both batch sizes are derivable, landing as ONE batched diff (swap + claim + two-batch branch + computed constants). **Center-of-gravity rationale (where a requirement spans design + impl + test + close):**

- **AFF-01 / AFF-02** (the affiliate distribution — the flat-7% deterministic-split PULL: accrue flat 7% per buy into the running `affiliateBase`, settle by PULL via `claim`/`withdraw` with the fixed 75/20/5 split [no roll, no seed, no scheduled/mutation affiliate flush]; taper afking-N/A + leaderboard-at-claim [_amended 2026-06-01 — flat-7% deterministic-split pull; quests stay automatic: SUPERSEDES the XMODEL roll-unification, the roll is removed_]) → SPEC (353), where they are DESIGN-LOCKED as the load-bearing non-gameability decisions BEFORE any code (the affiliate distribution mechanism IS a design choice, not a built behavior — once the flat-7%-accrue / deterministic-split-PULL shape is locked, IMPL builds it inside the aggregator). The aggregator + the affiliate PULL that USE them (AGG-01..05 + the `claim`/`withdraw` plumbing) are owned at IMPL; AFF-01/02 are the distribution-mechanism design that the affiliate accrue + the QUEST-only AGG-02/03 settle consume — no double-counting (AGG = the quest accrue/settle plumbing + the affiliate accrue; AFF = the distribution rule the `claim` PULL applies).
- **XMODEL-01** (the cross-model Codex + Gemini review) → SPEC (353) as its HOME, because its PRIMARY deliverable is the DESIGN-INPUT pass that must be folded into the design-lock BEFORE IMPL (the gating half — it shapes the mechanism). Its TERMINAL close-augmentation half (Codex + Gemini augmenting the Claude 3-skill sweep) is a touchpoint REFLECTED in Phase 357's success criteria (AUDIT-01's sweep), NOT a separate requirement count — the instruction's "assign it to the phase where its primary deliverable lands … but reflect both touchpoints" resolved to SPEC-as-home.
- **AGG-01..05 · TKT-01/02 · QST-01..05 · OPEN-01/02** (the built behaviors) → IMPL (354) as part of the single batched diff. The SPEC concerns those decisions feed (the accumulator layout, the ticket-primitive shape, the `DegenerusQuests` batched-settle entrypoint shape + non-perturbation approach, the ±10-streak derivation, the open-end review) are folded into the SPEC's success criteria (SC2/SC3/SC4) — they are NOT double-counted at SPEC; only the requirement's HOME (where it must be BUILT) is counted at IMPL.
- **GAS-01 / GAS-02 / GAS-03 / GAS-04** (the measured everyday-cost reduction — per-buy/per-settle marginals, accumulator packing, `SUB_STAGE_BATCH` re-tune, mode/SLOAD collapse) → GAS (355). Note: much of GAS-01/02 is structural to the IMPL refactor (the cheap accrue + the deferred settle + the packed accumulator ARE the saving); the GAS phase MEASURES the savings (proven same-results in TST), lands the residual `SUB_STAGE_BATCH` re-tune + the mode/SLOAD collapse, and gates any net contract change under the same USER-approved diff (or records Outcome-A no-diff per the v55 350 precedent). The SPEC produces the accumulator-layout decision (folded into SC2), but the wins LAND/are measured at the GAS phase.
- **SEC-01 / SEC-02** (the hard security floor — unmanipulable esp. strategic sub/unsub; SOLVENCY-01 untouched + RNG-freeze intact) → TST (356), where they are PROVEN empirically + adversarially as the hard gate (per the explicit "TST Owns SEC-01/02" directive — mirrors v55, where FREEZE design lived at SPEC but the empirical proofs were a distinct phase). The SPEC "SEC design" (the unmanipulable/solvency/freeze re-attestation on paper) is the design gate folded into 353's SC5 — NOT a separate count; the TERMINAL adversarial review (AUDIT-01) is the FINAL gate that re-confirms SEC, but SEC-01/02's center-of-gravity (where the property is first PROVEN, incl. the strategic-sub/unsub proof) is TST. No double-counting.
- **AUDIT-01** (the TERMINAL FULL close) → TERMINAL (357); it re-attests all 24 v56.0 requirements + runs the in-milestone delta-audit + the 3-skill adversarial sweep AUGMENTED by the XMODEL cross-model close + `audit/FINDINGS-v56.0.md` + the atomic 5-doc closure flip with the `MILESTONE_V56_AT_HEAD_<sha>` signal.
